```text

```

This loop adds **48** new R13 cross-pattern representative cases, **31** counterexamples/residual cases, and **42** current-profile residual errors for **R13 / L10_POLICY_EVENT_CROSS_REDTEAM_MISC / R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM**.

R13 is the circuit breaker panel, not another sector room. It reuses the completed Loop 15 R1~R12 historical rows and asks whether the same wiring fault appears across unrelated archetypes: headline-only Stage2 promotion, price-only local 4B, late hard 4C, accounting/trust breaks, and high-MAE winners that should remain eligible when non-price evidence survives.

## 1. Current Calibrated Profile Assumption

```text
current_default_profile_proxy = e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated_proxy
previous_baseline_reference = e2r_2_0_baseline_reference
stage2_actionable_evidence_bonus = +2.0
stage3_yellow_total_min = 75.0
stage3_green_total_min = 87.0
stage3_green_revision_min = 55.0
stage3_cross_evidence_green_buffer = +1.5
price_only_blowoff_blocks_positive_stage = true
full_4b_requires_non_price_evidence = true
hard_4c_thesis_break_routes_to_4c = true
```

This file does not patch production scoring. The already-applied global axes are stress-tested, not re-proved. The proposed rows are shadow-only and scoped to the R13 cross-archetype router.

## 3. Previous Coverage / Duplicate Avoidance Check

Local continuation contains Loop 15 R1~R12 source MDs. The immediately preceding run completed R12 / Loop 15 and pointed to R13 / Loop 15. A current repository search did not find an existing `e2r_stock_web_v12_residual_round_R13_loop_15` file, so this file resolves to R13 / Loop 15 and passes the schedule gate.

## 4. Stock-Web OHLC Input / Price Source Validation

```text
source_name = FinanceData/marcap
source_repo_url = https://github.com/FinanceData/marcap
price_adjustment_status = raw_unadjusted_marcap
min_date = 1995-05-02
max_date = 2026-02-20
tradable_row_count = 14354401
raw_row_count = 15214118
symbol_count = 5414
active_like_symbol_count = 2868
inactive_or_delisted_like_symbol_count = 2546
markets = KONEX | KOSDAQ | KOSDAQ GLOBAL | KOSPI
calibration_shard_root = atlas/ohlcv_tradable_by_symbol_year
raw_shard_root = atlas/ohlcv_raw_by_symbol_year
schema_path = atlas/schema.json
universe_path = atlas/universe/all_symbols.csv
price_basis = tradable_raw
```

The selected R13 rows are actual trigger-level rows emitted by the R1~R12 Loop 15 MDs, each originally calculated from Songdaiki/stock-web OHLC shards. Each selected trigger retains `price_shard_path`, `profile_path`, `entry_date`, `entry_price`, MFE/MAE fields, corporate-action status, and `stock_web_manifest_max_date = 2026-02-20`. The atlas is raw/unadjusted; corporate-action-contaminated windows remain blocked or narrative-only.

## 5. Historical Eligibility Gate

```text
trigger_count_total = 68
calibration_usable_trigger_count = 68
representative_trigger_count = 47
case_count_total = 48
forward_window_basis = stock_web_manifest_max_date, not current calendar date
corporate_action_window_policy = clean_180D_window required for quantitative calibration
```

All quantitative rows included here inherit the source Loop 15 validation fields. Any row with insufficient forward window, missing price fields, or corporate-action contamination would remain narrative-only and would not enter the aggregate. In this R13 file, all machine-readable trigger rows are calibration-usable in the source rows.

## 6. Canonical Archetype Compression Map

```text
R13_CROSS_ARCHETYPE_4B_4C_REDTEAM compresses these source archetypes:
- C05_EPC_MEGA_CONTRACT_MARGIN_GAP: 6 cases
- C06_HBM_MEMORY_CUSTOMER_CAPACITY: 3 cases
- C14_EV_DEMAND_SLOWDOWN_4B_4C: 3 cases
- C16_STRATEGIC_RESOURCE_POLICY_SUPPLY: 3 cases
- C20_BEAUTY_FOOD_GLOBAL_DISTRIBUTION: 3 cases
- C21_FINANCIAL_ROE_PBR_CAPITAL_RETURN: 3 cases
- C23_BIO_REGULATORY_APPROVAL_COMMERCIALIZATION: 3 cases
- C26_PLATFORM_AD_REVENUE_OPERATING_LEVERAGE: 3 cases
- C29_MOBILITY_VOLUME_MARGIN_OPERATING_LEVERAGE: 4 cases
- C30_CONSTRUCTION_PF_BALANCE_SHEET_BREAK: 4 cases
- C31_POLICY_SUBSIDY_LEGISLATION_EVENT: 8 cases
- C32_GOVERNANCE_CONTROL_PREMIUM_TENDER_CAP: 5 cases
```

Compression rule: the source archetype explains the business mechanism; the R13 router explains the failure mode. A false Stage2 in a platform company and a false Stage2 in a policy proxy are different rooms, but the wiring fault is the same if headline beta replaces non-price evidence.

## 8. Positive vs Counterexample Balance

```text
positive_case_count = 17
counterexample_count = 31
current_profile_error_count = 42
minimum_positive_case_count = 1 -> pass
minimum_counterexample_count = 1 -> pass
minimum_calibration_usable_case_count = 3 -> pass
```

The file is deliberately counterexample-heavy. Its job is not to add another sector-specific bullish rule; it stress-tests how a calibrated profile behaves when price action, event hype, and true thesis evidence are braided together.

## 13. Current Calibrated Profile Stress Test

```text
current_profile_false_positive_case_count = 17
current_profile_missed_or_late_case_count = 12
current_profile_4B_error_trigger_count = 11
current_profile_4C_error_trigger_count = 8
current_profile_error_trigger_count = 55
```

Answer to the required stress questions:

1. The current calibrated profile would correctly block many price-only blowoffs, but still lets some headline-only Stage2/Green cases through when the source archetype has a plausible story but lacks a non-price bridge.
2. Actual MFE/MAE is mixed: structural winners exist, but the false-positive cluster has shallow MFE and deep MAE.
3. The Stage2 actionable bonus is not globally wrong; it is too generous when evidence is public-event beta without contract, customer, revision, margin, or accounting quality confirmation.
4. Yellow threshold 75 is broadly kept. The residual problem is evidence composition, not a single threshold.
5. Green threshold 87 / revision 55 is kept, but Green should remain blocked where source rows show price-only or narrative-only rerating.
6. The price-only blowoff guard is strengthened.
7. The full 4B non-price requirement is strengthened: a local price peak can be overlay-only, not a full cycle exit, unless non-price risk confirms.
8. Hard 4C routing is strengthened where accounting, safety, regulatory rejection, order cut, or thesis break evidence exists; waiting for price collapse makes 4C late.

## 14. Stage2 / Yellow / Green Comparison

The cross-row result is mechanical: Stage2 and Yellow work best when they are like a bridge with two beams—price action on one side, non-price evidence on the other. When one beam is missing, the same label becomes a plank over air.

```text
stage2_actionable_evidence_bonus = existing_axis_kept_but_composition_guard_needed
stage3_yellow_total_min = existing_axis_kept
stage3_green_total_min = existing_axis_kept
stage3_green_revision_min = existing_axis_kept
stage3_cross_evidence_green_buffer = existing_axis_kept
new_cross_guard = non_price_bridge_required_for_positive_stage
```

## 15. 4B Local vs Full-window Timing Audit

```text
avg_four_b_local_peak_proximity = 0.66
avg_four_b_full_window_peak_proximity = 0.63
full_4B_requires_non_price_evidence = existing_axis_strengthened
price_only_local_peak_policy = overlay_only_not_full_exit
```

Rows with price-only or positioning-only 4B evidence are retained as overlay/risk rows. They do not by themselves rewrite the source thesis into full 4B or hard 4C.

## 16. 4C Protection Audit

Hard 4C is useful when the evidence is not merely that price fell, but that the thesis broke: safety/trust failure, regulatory rejection, accounting distrust, contract/order failure, or forced liquidity route. Loop 15 contains multiple cases where hard 4C was late under the current profile; R13 therefore proposes a router rather than a lower price threshold.

```text
hard_4c_thesis_break_routes_to_4c = existing_axis_strengthened
4C_late_error_count = 6
4C_early_error_count = 2
```

## 17. Sector-Specific Rule Candidate

```text
sector_specific_rule_candidate = false
reason = R13 is cross-archetype checkpoint, not a sector room.
```

## 18. Canonical-Archetype Rule Candidate

```text
canonical_archetype_rule_candidate = true
rule_scope = R13_cross_archetype_router
proposal = NON_PRICE_BRIDGE_REQUIRED_FOR_POSITIVE_STAGE | LOCAL_4B_OVERLAY_NOT_FULL_EXIT | HARD_4C_THESIS_BREAK_ROUTER | HIGH_MAE_STRUCTURAL_SURVIVOR_EXCEPTION
```

Proposed shadow router:

- Positive Stage2/Yellow/Green requires at least one non-price bridge: contract/customer quality, revision, margin bridge, accounting trust, regulatory approval, capital-return visibility, or direct demand/capacity route.
- Price-only local peak is 4B overlay-only unless non-price overhang, valuation blowoff, dilution, delay, legal block, margin slowdown, or positioning evidence is present.
- Hard 4C is triggered by thesis-break evidence, not by waiting for the chart to confess after the damage is done.
- High MAE does not automatically invalidate a structural winner when the non-price bridge remains intact.

## 19. Before / After Backtest Comparison

|profile_id|profile_scope|eligible_trigger_count|avg_MFE_90D_pct|avg_MAE_90D_pct|avg_MFE_180D_pct|avg_MAE_180D_pct|false_positive_rate|missed_structural_count|late_green_count|avg_four_b_local_peak_proximity|avg_four_b_full_window_peak_proximity|score_return_alignment_verdict|
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
|e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated_proxy|R13_cross_archetype_shadow_only|47|37.69|-22.98|45.91|-28.37|0.354|12|16|0.66|0.63|mixed: residual false positives and missed structural winners remain|
|e2r_2_0_baseline_reference|R13_cross_archetype_shadow_only|47|37.69|-22.98|45.91|-28.37|0.534|10|20|0.66|0.63|worse false positive control; useful only as rollback reference|
|r13_existing_axis_stress_profile|R13_cross_archetype_shadow_only|47|37.69|-22.98|45.91|-28.37|0.354|12|16|0.66|0.63|existing axes are directionally right but not granular enough by archetype|
|r13_cross_archetype_guard_profile|R13_cross_archetype_shadow_only|47|37.69|-22.98|45.91|-28.37|0.134|8|10|0.66|0.63|best balance; reduces false positives while preserving non-price high-MAE survivors|
|r13_counterexample_guard_profile|R13_cross_archetype_shadow_only|47|37.69|-22.98|45.91|-28.37|0.054|15|13|0.66|0.63|safer but risks missing legitimate high-MAE structural winners|

## 20. Score-Return Alignment Matrix

```text
score_return_alignment_verdict = mixed_before_cross_router / improved_under_R13_shadow_router
main_residual = evidence composition, not raw threshold
best_supported_profile = P2_r13_cross_archetype_guard_profile
```

The returned pattern is a common calibration trap: a stock can look right for the wrong reason, and another can look wrong before the thesis proves right. R13 therefore routes by evidence durability rather than by the first price burst.

## 26. Deferred Coding Agent Handoff Prompt

### Purpose

You are now in the repository implementation phase. The attached Markdown files are v12 post-calibrated residual research outputs produced using the Songdaiki/stock-web OHLC atlas.

These MDs are not live candidate research. They are historical calibration research designed to extend the already-applied e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated profile.

Do not blindly apply every shadow row. Ingest the machine-readable rows and update the sector/canonical-archetype calibration ledger.

### Price source context

- Primary historical price source used by the research MD: Songdaiki/stock-web.
- Price basis: tradable_raw.
- Price adjustment status: raw_unadjusted_marcap.
- Price shard pattern: atlas/ohlcv_tradable_by_symbol_year/<prefix>/<ticker>/<year>.csv.
- Symbol profile pattern: atlas/symbol_profiles/<prefix>/<ticker>.json.

### Rules

- Use only calibration_usable=true rows for quantitative calibration.
- Do not count reused cases as new independent evidence unless independent_evidence_weight > 0.
- Do not treat schema_rematerialization_only or duplicate_low_value_loop as new evidence.
- Do not apply global deltas unless multiple large_sector_id values support the same direction.
- Prefer sector_specific or canonical_archetype_specific shadow profiles.
- Positive score promotion requires non-price evidence and clean 180D MFE/MAE.
- 4B rows are overlay/risk calibration only.
- 4C rows are thesis-break/protection calibration only.
- price-only rows cannot promote Stage2/Stage3.
- If a v12 MD weakens an already applied axis, log it as residual counterexample rather than immediately reverting.
- Production scoring must not change unless the user explicitly asks for another promotion batch.

### Expected repository tasks

1. Parse case / trigger / score_simulation / shadow_weight / residual_contribution rows.
2. Validate stock-web price source fields.
3. Validate large_sector_id and canonical_archetype_id.
4. Validate novelty and reuse fields.
5. Deduplicate same_entry_group_id and reused cases.
6. Aggregate by large_sector_id and canonical_archetype_id.
7. Update sector_shadow_profile and archetype_shadow_profile only.
8. Preserve global calibrated profile unless explicitly promoted.
9. Report new independent cases, counterexamples, and residual error types.
10. Add tests that duplicate low-value loops cannot change weights.

### Expected output

- Concise implementation summary.
- Rows accepted/rejected.
- New sector/canonical archetype coverage.
- Existing axis strengthened/weakened/kept.
- No investment recommendation language.
